### 5. 逼真的纹身自拍肖像（结构化 JSON）

**Author**: [KeorUnreal](https://x.com/KeorUnreal)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 一个详细、结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于生成一张逼真的年轻女性特写自拍照，她身上有大量纹身。提示词指定了拍摄对象的另类风格，包括一条白色牛仔背带裙，其中一根肩带滑落，露出胸部和手臂上的大面积纹身。场景设定在一个舒适、植物环绕的室内客厅，环境光线温暖，强调纹身线条和色彩的清晰度。

![逼真的纹身自拍肖像（结构化 JSON）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063168050_j02hz2_G_NUON7XkAAT8aB.jpg)
![逼真的纹身自拍肖像（结构化 JSON）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063168042_p4ck39_G_NUOJ5WsAAJWD8.jpg)
![逼真的纹身自拍肖像（结构化 JSON）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063168085_zrd8u5_G_NUODYX0AAeYaP.jpg)
![逼真的纹身自拍肖像（结构化 JSON）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063168787_b192jg_G_NUOMJXQAAsweA.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_type": "photorealistic selfie portrait",
  "main_composition": "close-up selfie view of a single young woman holding her phone at arm's length, looking directly at the camera with a subtle confident expression, one strap of her overall dress unfastened and slipped down her shoulder revealing extensive chest and arm tattoos, relaxed casual pose in a cozy plant-filled indoor living space, warm ambient lighting with lush greenery and furniture in soft blurred background",
  "subject": {
    "description": "beautiful young woman in her early 20s, attractive feminine features with bold alternative makeup (sharp dark winged eyeliner, long lashes, contoured cheeks, glossy nude or pink lips), large expressive eyes, fair smooth skin with healthy glow, long loose wavy dark brown or black hair with natural volume and slight tousle falling over shoulders",
    "clothing": "white denim overall mini dress with delicate small floral print throughout, thin straps with metal buckles—one strap intentionally unfastened and slipped off shoulder exposing upper chest, no visible top underneath",
    "details": "extensive visible colorful tattoos including large floral dagger/rose design on chest, detailed traditional style flowers and patterns on both full arms and hands, small neck tattoo, silver septum nose ring, manicured hands with dark painted nails holding phone, confident subtle pout or smile with direct eye contact, hair naturally wavy with soft strands framing face"
  },
  "environment": {
    "foreground": "woman's arms and phone in sharp focus, visible tattoo details",
    "midground": "woman centered in frame",
    "background": "cozy modern indoor living room or sunroom filled with lush green houseplants (monstera, trailing vines, potted varieties), dark couch with yellow pillow on left, wooden elements and warm ambient lighting suggesting relaxed home atmosphere, no clutter in focus"
  },
  "lighting_and_atmosphere": "warm soft indoor ambient lighting (likely from off-frame window or lamps) creating gentle golden glow on skin, hair, white denim fabric, and tattoo colors, subtle shadows enhancing facial contours and body curves, intimate casual confident vibe with high contrast between bright subject and darker cozy background, photorealistic detail evoking relaxed alternative beauty",
  "technical_quality": "highly detailed, sharp focus on tattoo ink colors and linework, denim fabric texture with floral print, hair strands, skin glow, nose ring reflection, and phone case details, 8k resolution, realistic material sheen on denim and subtle makeup details, professional selfie photography style with natural depth of field softly blurring background plants and furniture",
  "negative_prompt_suggestions": "blurry, deformed, extra limbs, harsh flash lighting, overexposed skin, underexposed tattoos, low quality, cartoon, anime, text water
```

[[Warm Ambient Light]] [[Alternative Aesthetic]]

### 6. 20 世纪 80 年代地下书呆子技术派对闪光照片提示

**Author**: [TechHalla](https://x.com/techhalla)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 生成一张逼真的抓拍闪光照片的提示词，模仿 20 世纪 80 年代地下书呆子技术派对的场景。它需要使用一张上传的图片来呈现主要人物的面部和鲻鱼头，该人物戴着百叶窗眼镜，在烟雾弥漫的昏暗地下迪斯科舞厅里，一群“不酷”的 80 年代书呆子中间尽情跳舞。

![20 世纪 80 年代地下书呆子技术派对闪光照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063188585_petjtv_G_NQWc_WsAAhozk.jpg)
![20 世纪 80 年代地下书呆子技术派对闪光照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063188666_86am1v_G_NQXWIWcAAeycb.jpg)
![20 世纪 80 年代地下书呆子技术派对闪光照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063188639_s8jasd_G_NQYFQW0AAXJ_Q.jpg)
![20 世纪 80 年代地下书呆子技术派对闪光照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063190199_qw547z_G_NQY7KWEAASnZK.jpg)

```
DIRECTIVE: A photorealistic, candid flash photo from a 1980s underground nerd techno party.

SUBJECT/CHARACTER:
  CRITICAL: Use attached image/video as strict reference for the man's face and mullet hair.
  ACCESSORY: He is wearing white or neon plastic shutter shade sunglasses (horizontal slats).
  EXPRESSION: Mouth slightly open, mid-dance move, looking intense.

SCENE & LAYOUT:
  Environment: A dark, smoke-filled basement disco with cheap laser lights.
  CROWD (Background): A diverse group of "uncool" 80s geeks. Overweight guys with suspenders, skinny girls with frizzy hair and braces, people in homemade "Tron" or "Star Wars" costumes made of foil.
  Action: Everyone is dancing awkwardly to techno music.

TECHNICAL SPECS:
  Camera: 35mm point-and-shoot camera with direct on-camera flash.
  Style: Vintage candid snapshot, high contrast, slight motion blur on the background dancers.
  Vibe: Geek culture, "Freaks and Geeks," authentic 80s awkwardness.
```

[[Retro Aesthetic]]

### 8. 超写实高端时尚坐姿肖像提示词

**Author**: [maniBuildsAI](https://x.com/manibuildsAI)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术性的提示，用于生成一张超现实、摄影测量的曲线女性肖像，她坐在一张极简主义的表面上。提示强调毛孔级别的皮肤细节、特定的头发保留（需要参考图像），以及详细的服装元素，如象牙色蕾丝迷你连衣裙和金属金色细高跟凉鞋，场景设定在一个高端的时尚摄影工作室中。

![超写实高端时尚坐姿肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063203835_gxq2xt_G_NCzoqaIAEaL3p.jpg)
![超写实高端时尚坐姿肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063204465_0ucfq2_G_NCzuKaQAA2IWB.jpg)
![超写实高端时尚坐姿肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063204518_kmxlac_G_NCz6PW0AAh1ye.jpg)

```
{
  "project_metadata": {
    "version": "2.0",
    "target_quality": "Hyper-Realistic / Photogrammetric",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
    "reference_parameters": {
      "identity_preservation": "High (Strictly maintain facial geometry and hairstyle from reference image)",
      "facial_integrity": "Unmodified facial features, zero distortion"
    }
  },
  "subject_details": {
    "human_attributes": {
      "physique": "Curvy, well-defined silhouette",
      "skin_texture": "Pore-level detail, natural skin sheen, realistic subsurface scattering",
      "gaze": "Direct eye contact with camera, engaging and confident expression"
    },
    "hair_specification": {
      "style": "Exact match to attached photo",
      "texture": "Fine strands, realistic sheen, high-fidelity fiber rendering",
      "interaction": "Naturally draped based on the seated pose"
    },
    "pose_composition": {
      "action": "Seated on a minimalist surface",
      "orientation": "Torso leaning slightly forward toward the lens",
      "lower_body": "Legs crossed and elevated/raised to foreground",
      "focal_emphasis": "Emphasis on leg length and high-heeled footwear"
    }
  },
  "wardrobe_and_styling": {
    "primary_garment": {
      "item": "Minidress",
      "color": "Ivory / Off-white",
      "material": "Silk or satin base with intricate lace overlay",
      "design_elements": [
        "Delicate spaghetti straps",
        "Subtle 3D floral embroidery",
        "Fine lace scalloped edges",
        "Form-fitting curvy silhouette"
      ]
    },
    "footwear": {
      "type": "Stiletto high-heeled sandals",
      "finish": "Metallic gold, reflective",
      "fastening": "Delicate ankle straps with micro-buckle detail",
      "presentation": "Polished, catching the studio light"
    },
    "accessories": {
      "earrings": "Small minimalist gold studs or hoops",
      "jewelry_tone": "Warm metallic gold"
    }
  },
  "environment_and_lighting": {
    "setting": "High-end minimalist studio or neutral architectural background",
    "lighting_setup": {
      "primary": "Softbox key light for even skin tones",
      "secondary": "Subtle rim lighting to define the body curves and hair texture",
      "ambience": "Clean, sophisticated, high-fashion editorial aesthetic"
    },
    "color_palette": [
      "Ivory",
      "Warm Gold",
      "Neutral Skin Tones",
      "Soft Muted Background"
    ]
  },
  "technical_render_specs": {
    "camera": {
      "lens": "85mm prime lens (portrait specialty)",
      "aperture": "f/2.8 for sharp subject focus and soft background blur",
      "sensor": "Full-frame CMOS",
      "shot_type": "Full body / Medium shot"
    },
    "resolution_quality": [
      "8k UHD",
      "Highly detailed textures",
      "Ray-traced reflections on metallic surfaces",
      "Masterpiece quality"
    ]
  }
}
```

### 9. 科学领域研究员的文档板提示

**Author**: [Alexandra Aisling](https://x.com/AllaAisling)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一个多部分文档板，模仿野外研究人员的研究。它需要一张科学插图、一张生态背景地图，以及一张拍摄对象在其自然栖息地中的照片，融合了临床、制图和《国家地理》的风格。

![科学领域研究员的文档板提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063173711_oz6u5l_G_M6E2MWQAUsAka.jpg)
![科学领域研究员的文档板提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063173727_8g7olc_G_M50VuWQAE_9Ye.jpg)
![科学领域研究员的文档板提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063173887_oon8ko_G_M6RxqWQAQmxrg.jpg)
![科学领域研究员的文档板提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063175173_sgac5s_G_M6a1XWQAArO3z.jpg)

```
A field researcher's documentation board for {argument name="animal or plant" default="[ANIMAL / PLANT / ORGANISM]"} — {argument name="scientific name" default="[SCIENTIFIC NAME / HABITAT]"}. Left section: scientific illustration showing anatomical details, life-cycle stages, or seasonal variation, with measurement scales and taxonomic classification. Center section: ecological context map showing range, habitat preferences, predator-prey relationships, and conservation status indicators. Right section: the subject in its natural habitat, captured in a decisive moment, behavior visible, environment authentic, the data made alive. Visual style transitions from specimen-drawer clinical through cartographic neutrals to National Geographic field photography. Title block reading "{argument name="common name" default="[COMMON NAME]"} — [SCIENTIFIC NAME], [CONSERVATION STATUS], FIELD STUDY [YEAR]".
```

[[Documentary Photography]] [[Scientific Illustration]] [[National Geographic Style]]

### 10. 2x2 名人照相亭网格提示

**Author**: [Qaiser Tzq](https://x.com/TzqQaiser)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化提示，详细描述了生成一张 2x2 拍立得照片网格，其中包含安娜·德·阿玛斯（Ana de Armas）和西德尼·斯威尼（Sydney Sweeney），并具体说明了她们的服装、发型以及每个象限的四种不同的俏皮互动/姿势（例如，运动姿势、背人、摇滚主题）。

![2x2 名人照相亭网格提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063229818_9r1vuj_G_M5OchbkAEOGxo.jpg)

```
{

  "project": "Celebrity_Photo_Booth_Analysis_2026",
  "metadata": {
    "composition_type": "2x2 Image Grid",
    "background_color_hex": "#4A708B",
    "lighting": "Soft Studio Lighting / Flash",
    "subject_count": 2
  },
  "subjects": [
    {
      "id": "subject_01",
      "name": "Ana de Armas",
      "physical_attributes": {
        "hair_color": "Brunette",
        "hair_style": "Wavy, Shoulder-length",
        "outfit": "Black sequined sleeveless mini-dress/top",
        "accessories": "Small silver earrings"
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "subject_02",
      "name": "Sydney Sweeney",
      "physical_attributes": {
        "hair_color": "Blonde",
        "hair_style": "Short bob, wavy",
        "outfit": "Silver/Platinum satin floor-length gown",
        "outfit_detail": "Jeweled/Crystal straps",
        "accessories": "Thin silver necklace"
      }
    }
  ],
  "detailed_grid_breakdown": {
    "quadrant_1_top_left": {
      "interaction": "Athletic Pose",
      "ana_de_armas": {
        "pose": "Bicep flex with both arms",
        "gaze": "Direct to camera",
        "mood": "Playful/Strong"
      },
      "sydney_sweeney": {
        "pose": "Leaning forward, hands out of frame",
        "gaze": "Direct to camera",
        "mood": "Candid/Action"
      }
    },
    "quadrant_2_top_right": {
      "interaction": "Close-up Intimacy",
      "ana_de_armas": {
        "pose": "Bending low, hands on knees",
        "expression": "Sultry/Engaged",
        "focus": "High-angle perspective"
      },
      "sydney_sweeney": {
        "pose": "Head tilted, arm framing the top",
        "expression": "Soft smile",
        "focus": "Side-profile/Frontal mix"
      }
    },
    "quadrant_3_bottom_left": {
      "interaction": "Piggyback / Friendship Bond",
      "action_detail": "Sydney is carrying Ana on her back",
      "ana_de_armas": {
        "pose": "Arms wrapped around Sydney's neck",
        "expression": "Ecstatic laughter",
        "teeth_visible": true
      },
      "sydney_sweeney": {
        "pose": "Supporting Ana's legs, leaning back",
        "expression": "Genuine joy/Laughter",
        "teeth_visible": true
      }
    },
    "quadrant_4_bottom_right": {
      "interaction": "Funny / Rock-themed",
      "ana_de_armas": {
        "pose": "Leaning sharply to the left side",
        "expression": "Pout / Duck face",
        "vibe": "Silly"
      },
      "sydney_sweeney": {
        "pose": "Standing upright in the back",
        "expression": "Deadpan / Serious face",
        "hand_gestures": "Double 'Sign of the Horns' (🤟)"
      }
    }
  ],
  "overall_aesthetic": {
    "color_palette": ["Steel Blue", "Silver", "Midnight Black"],
    "emotional_tags": ["Fun", "Glamorous", "Sisterhood", "Energetic"]
  }
}
```

### 12. 超现实的吉卜力工作室美食广告提示

**Author**: [Meem](https://x.com/mehvishs25)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成超现实的 1:1 食物广告（品客薯片）的提示。它要求将超逼真的食物放置在一个随机选择的、受吉卜力工作室启发的梦幻场景中（例如，漂浮在天空中的市场），使食物看起来充满魔力，并带有“风味光环”，同时包含一句富有诗意的标语。

![超现实的吉卜力工作室美食广告提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063190833_771d6o_G_Myqg8bcAA8X86.jpg)

```
Create a surreal 1:1 advertisement for [{argument name="brand name" default="Pringles"}], placing the hyper-realistic food item in a randomly selected dreamlike setting inspired by Studio Ghibli.
The background could be a floating sky market, a glowing metro station, a whimsical old alley, or a forest shrine in twilight — let the environment match the soul of the brand.
The food must appear vibrant, magical, and emit a soft ‘flavor aura’.
Include a poetic slogan that fits the mood.
Style: cinematic, painterly background, Studio Ghibli vibes, photorealistic food, high detail, soft atmospheric lighting.
```

[[Studio Ghibli Aesthetic]]

![高质量全身时尚摄影提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063209323_dz3wb9_G_MyairW0AA3CVg.jpg)

```
Use the same face from the reference image without changing facial features 

{
  "action": "image_generation",
  "input_text": "A high-quality full-body photograph of a smiling western woman with glowing tan skin sitting on clean white indoor stairs. She is wearing a stylish patterned headscarf in shades of {argument name="headscarf colors" default="pink, black, and white"}, paired with large gold hoop earrings. Her outfit consists of a dark patterned tank top and a flowing black skirt with a high slit. She has visible tattoos on both shoulders and red manicured nails. The lighting is warm and soft, creating a bright and minimalist aesthetic against the solid white architectural background."
}

**Author**: [K](https://x.com/ChillaiKalan__)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 将上传图像转换为一张高冲击力、超现实的东欧男性数字插画的复杂提示。它要求 100% 的面部识别匹配，特色是大胆的橙色反光太阳镜，镜片中倒映着城市景观，并使用柔和的灰度色调与霓虹绿和电蓝色抽象画笔笔触形成对比。

![超现实电影级数字插画提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063225543_rpqzbo_G_MyA0yXAAEARMl.jpg)

```
Transform the uploaded image into a high-impact digital illustration using the image as a strict facial reference. Face Match (Strict): Face match must remain 100% exact — identical facial structure, proportions, jawline, cheekbones, nose shape, lips, beard density(if available in reference image) and trim, skin texture, hairline, hairstyle, and overall identity. Do not beautify, stylize, or alter facial features. Subject & Pose: A young Eastern European man is shown in a clean side-profile pose (not extreme profile), facing toward the right side of the frame. His head is slightly raised, chin gently lifted, conveying confidence, ambition, and forward vision. Expression is calm and self-assured. Clothing & Styling: The subject wears formal, modern clothing — a tailored dark blazer over a crisp shirt, minimal and elegant, reinforcing a professional and ambitious persona. No distracting accessories. Key Visual Element: He wears bold orange reflective sunglasses as the focal point. The lenses reflect a detailed modern cityscape with skyscrapers, urban roads, and green trees, symbolizing vision, ambition, and future goals. Color & Illustration Style: The face and clothing are rendered in muted grayscale tones, with realistic texture translated into a refined digital illustration style. Surrounding the subject are expressive abstract paint strokes and splashes in neon green and electric blue, adding energy and contrast without covering facial details. Background & Lighting: The background is dark and dramatic, layered with deep grey tones, subtle texture, and painterly motion. Cinematic lighting creates strong subject separation, clean highlights, and controlled shadows. Overall Aesthetic: Modern, cinematic, surreal digital illustration with a 2/3 photoreal-illustration balance and 1/3 abstract expression, poster-quality, high contrast, premium look. Aspect Ratio: 4:5
```

### 22. 教育商品宇宙立体模型提示

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 一个教育性的、高度结构化的提示模板，旨在生成一个“商品宇宙”立体模型等距桌面摄影图像。它指示 AI 将选定的商品（如咖啡或黄金）解构为其核心、种类和历史运输方式，并将它们布置在一个抛光的木板上，以详细的博物馆风格展示。

![教育商品宇宙立体模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063198703_3k4ai0_G_ERfQVXgAAaud_.jpg)
![教育商品宇宙立体模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063198723_xmw01v_G_ERhPUW4AAo_mG.jpg)

```
<instruction> for {argument name="commodity" default="Coffee"}

Input A is a Historic Commodity or Resource (e.g., Spices, Tea, Silk, Coffee, Gold).
Deconstruct the commodity into 3 Educational Assets:
     The Core :  Identify the most common or valuable raw form.
         (e.g., Spices -> A pile of Black Peppercorns. Tea -> A mound of Black Tea leaves. Gold -> A large Nugget). 
     The Varieties:  Identify 4-5 distinct variations or colors.
         (e.g., Spices -> Red Paprika, Yellow Turmeric, Brown Cinnamon. Tea -> Green, White, Oolong, Matcha). 
     The Transit :  Identify the historical method of transport.
         (e.g., Camel Caravans, East Indiaman Ships, Steam Trains). 

  2. Container
Goal: "Commodity Universe" Educational Diorama.
     The Base:  A large, square   Polished Walnut or Oak Board   sitting on a library table.
     The Layout:  A radial/circular design in the center, flanked by narrative vignettes in the corners.

  3. The Centerpiece
     The Metaphor:  The commodity is the center of the world.
     The Sun:  A massive, textured pile of the "Core" material (Step 1) sits in the exact center.
     The Orbit:  Inlaid gold or brass rings ripple out from the center.
     The Planets:  Smaller mounds or spheres of the "Varieties" (Step 1) orbit the center, creating a colorful spectrum of textures (powders, grains, solids).

  4. Narrative Corners 
     The Origin (Top Corners):  Miniature dioramas sculpted directly onto the board showing the harvesting process (e.g., tiny figures picking tea leaves, mining gold, or shaking spice trees).
     The Journey (Bottom Corners):  Miniature dioramas showing the "Transit" (Step 1).
         Detail:  Use   Resin   for water (ships) or   Sand   for deserts (camels).

  5. The Footer:  
     Placement:  Along the bottom edge of the board.
     Format:  Three or four rectangular   Wooden Plaques   embedded in the table.
     Content:  The name of a specific variety (e.g., "Cinnamon") engraved in serif text, with a physical sample of that ingredient piled on the plaque.

  Output:   ONE image, 1:1 Aspect Ratio, Isometric Tabletop Photography, "Museum Display" aesthetic, Warm Tones.
</instruction>
```

[[Commodity Universe Diorama]]

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于在黑暗、迷人的夜生活环境中生成一张超逼真的编辑肖像。它要求直接使用机顶闪光灯，低环境背景，逼真的皮肤纹理（无修饰/AI 光泽），并指定了主体在天鹅绒包厢环境中的姿势和服装（黑色缎面迷你连衣裙）。

{
  "generation_request": {

      "no_logos": true,

    },

      "skin_rendering": "real_texture_no_retouch"
    },

      "camera_language": "direct on-camera flash, eye-level, intimate portrait, shallow depth of field",

    },
    "creative_prompt": {
      "scene_summary": "Glamorous nightlife portrait in a dark lounge or bar. Patterned velvet booth seating with animal/tiger print texture, warm wooden interior details in the background.",
      "subject": {
        "count": 1,
        "description": "young glamorous woman, confident and elegant",
        "expression": "soft confident gaze, slightly flirty, relaxed lips",

### 37. 动物和植物的烟花提示

**Author**: [ルナ｜使えるAI案内人](https://x.com/ai_skillmaster)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: ja

> 一个旨在生成将动物或植物描绘成正在发射的烟花的图像的提示。它支持指定颜色，并且可以通过文本输入（例如“rabbit”）或图像输入来触发。

![动物和植物的烟花提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063235121_mzfid4_G990wJxbcAYxubw.jpg)

```
動物や植物などを花火として打ち上げられるプロンプトです🎆
（NanoBanana Proでの使用がおすすめです）

今回は{argument name="色数" default="4色"}で表現していますが、単色や複数の色を指定することができます🌈

画像の添付だけでなく、{argument name="対象" default="ウサギ"}などの文字での指示でも対応してくれます😊
```

### 38. 高影响力产品爆炸视频提示

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的两场景提示，用于生成一个高冲击力的产品爆炸视频，其中一个红色番石榴汽水罐置于红色摄影棚背景前。场景 1 要求绝对静止，随后场景 2 立即要求番石榴液体和果肉剧烈、猛烈地爆裂，强调超现实的物理效果和爆炸性运动，没有电影般的柔和感。

![高影响力产品爆炸视频提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063212406_56yj47_G_KI828aoAMIal5.jpg)

```
A high-impact product explosion video featuring a red guava soda can centered in frame against a solid red studio background.

SCENE 1 — STILLNESS (0–3 seconds):
The soda can stands perfectly upright and completely still at the center of the frame. No liquid, no fruit, no motion. The can appears sealed, intact, and realistic with light condensation droplets. The background is clean and uniform red. Lighting is steady and neutral. No particles, no splashes, no anticipation effects. Absolute stillness is maintained for a full 3 seconds.

SCENE 2 — IMPACT BURST (instant after 3 seconds):
A violent guava splash erupts from behind the can at extreme speed. The splash is aggressive, sudden, and forceful — not cinematic, not slow motion. Thick red guava liquid explodes forward and upward, slamming into the back of the can and visibly shaking it.

Whole guavas, guava slices, and green leaves are launched outward with raw momentum, bursting through the empty space around the can. Liquid sheets tear through the air, creating sharp splashes, chaotic arcs, and dense droplets. The motion is fast, loud, and explosive.

The can remains mostly upright but reacts physically — shaking, vibrating, and slightly shifting from the impact. Fruit pieces and liquid fragments fill the frame by falling, colliding, and splashing around the can, occupying all previously empty space.

No elegance, no slow motion, no cinematic pacing. The burst feels uncontrolled, pressurized, and powerful. Lighting intensifies during the impact to emphasize liquid thickness, fruit texture, and high-speed motion. Final frames show suspended droplets, falling fruit, and liquid wrapping around the can in chaotic aftermath.

Ultra-realistic physics, extreme speed, aggressive energy, commercial-grade realism, bold contrast, explosive motion — no cinematic softness.
```

### 40. 日文文本生成比较 (Oha-you)

**Author**: [𝙐𝙨𝙖𝙢𝙞𝙠𝙤別館](https://x.com/usamiko286)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: ja

> 对 Nijijourney 和 Nano Banana 之间日语文本生成效果的比较，指出虽然像“おはよう”（早上好）这样的简单问候语可以正常使用，但更复杂的短语则不行，这表明可以采用一种工作流程，即使用 Nano Banana 来纠正或生成文本。

### 48. Nano Banana Pro 的卡通人物造型树提示

**Author**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的日式提示词，用于 Nano Banana Pro 创建一张真人大小的绿雕树的超逼真图像，该绿雕树以特定角色（棕色头发、双马尾、红眼睛、尖牙）为原型。绿雕树置于一个阳光斑驳、鲜花盛开的茂密花园环境中，背景是欧洲宫殿，采用垂直长宽比。

![Nano Banana Pro 的卡通人物造型树提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063243132_f5rxj5_G_Jw4p-aoAEkJ8E.jpg)

```
[キャラクター設定部分]
{argument name="キャラクター設定" default="茶色の髪、短いツインテール、赤い瞳、少し尖った歯（ギザ歯）"}。

[固定部分]
上記のキャラクターを模した、高さ2～3メートル程度の実物大トピアリー。
テーマパークの植え込みの中に設置されており、周囲の植物と一体化している。

足元と前景：
トピアリーの足元は、ピンク、紫、白などの色鮮やかなペチュニアやベゴニアのような花々で埋め尽くされている。土の地面は見えず、花の絨毯の中からトピアリーが立っているように見える。

周囲の環境と背景：
トピアリーのすぐ背後や横には、緑豊かな大きな広葉樹が植えられており、背景を覆っている。
広大な広場にポツンとあるのではなく、木々と花に囲まれた密度のある空間。
豪華でクラシックなヨーロッパ風の宮殿または大邸宅。建物はトピアリーの後ろに適切な距離感で配置されている。

光と影：
晴天。頭上の樹木を通した**「木漏れ日（Dappled sunlight）」**がトピアリーや足元の花壇に落ちており、実在感を強調している。

構図：
大人の目線の高さから、花壇越しに見上げるアングル。
手前の花々、中景のトピアリー、背景の樹木が重なり合い、奥行きと没入感がある。

スタイル：
高解像度の実写写真。鮮やかな色彩。8k、フォトリアル。

画像サイズ：
縦長（Vertical aspect ratio 9:16）

入力画像
アイコンの女の子

出力結果
```

[[Vertical Composition]] [[Fantasy Art]] [[Dappled Sunlight]]

```
A surreal minimalist conceptual artwork, a white light bulb with a large transparent glass sphere, glowing softly from inside with warm golden light at the bottom forming a gentle filament-like illumination. A small, delicate pure white bird ({argument name="bird type" default="white dove or small white sparrow"}) with subtle feather details perches calmly on the brightest inner glowing ring at the top of the filament inside the bulb. The light bulb is fused/merged seamlessly onto the upper torso of an elegant faceless white mannequin or abstract female figure dressed in a smooth minimalist white suit jacket with a high rolled white collar/stand collar. The figure is shown only from neck to waist in profile view, standing upright, clean elegant posture. The entire sculpture-like figure is pure white/ivory/off-white with soft matte ceramic or plaster texture. Very soft neutral gray studio background, subtle shadows, high-end surreal photography style, cinematic lighting, dreamlike peaceful atmosphere, conceptual art, extremely high detail, 8k resolution
```

### 63. 史诗级中国奇幻十二生肖神明提示词（12 个人物）

**Author**: [ttmouse - 豆爸](https://x.com/ttmouse)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: zh

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的极其详细、结构化的提示，旨在生成一幅史诗般的、超现实的电影卷轴，描绘十二生肖神祇（以人形出现）齐聚宏大的鸿蒙仙境。该提示指定了统一的世界观、8K 分辨率、电影质感，并详细说明了每个生肖如何由一个高价值的人形代表，其身后伴随着一个巨大的、半透明的“兽灵/武魂”光影投射，详细描述了所有 12 个人物的具体外观、服饰和位置。

![史诗级中国奇幻十二生肖神明提示词（12 个人物）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977347292_soddo8_G_IMtjBWQAAb32X.jpg)

```
真人本体+背后灵光虚像

全局风格与品质
视觉风格： 顶级写实修仙画卷，超现实电影级商业大片，硬核东方玄幻美学。
核心参数： 8K极高解析度，胶片质感，真实皮肤纹理（拒绝塑料感/二次元感）。
物理规则： 真实光影模拟，强调角色在特定环境下的重力与物理反馈。
构图策略： 超宽水平构图。十二位生肖化身处于同一片宏大的仙境时空中，从左至右错落排布，无视觉死角。
统一世界观： 场景设定在统一的“鸿蒙仙境”之中。环境从左侧的混沌灵脉逐渐过渡到右侧的云海仙踪。所有角色共享同一套大气光影，严禁生肖动物本体出现。

核心视觉特征
• 角色形态： 所有人均为极高颜值的真人形态，保留人类五官与肤质。
• 生肖体现： 通过角色的服饰剪裁、配色细节、随身法宝，以及角色背后由纯粹灵光构成的、宏大的“兽灵/武魂”虚像来体现生肖特征。
• 兽灵表现： 兽灵呈半透明光态或虚影态，完全由流动的灵气与辉光交织而成，不具备实体质感，如神迹般笼罩在角色后上方，充满神性。

摄影与光影
• 设备： 佳能 EOS R5, 35mm 定焦镜头。
• 光影设计： 统一受“仙境晨曦”照射，光线从画面一侧射入，形成丁达尔效应。
• 环境光补： 角色背后的兽灵光影散发着柔和的本命灵光，与仙境中的云雾、剑气相互折射。

角色分布与细节描述
1. 子鼠（水）： 极右侧云海。真人形态为灵动少年，墨色劲装，背后悬浮着如光般通透的硕大子鼠虚像，眼神机警。
2. 丑牛（土）： 沉稳壮汉，身披暗铜重甲。身后耸立着如山岳般的青牛光影虚像，展现力拔山河之势。
3. 寅虎（木）： 霸气统帅，黑金虎纹长袍。背后是一尊光影流转、似要下山的猛虎灵光虚像。
4. 卯兔（木）： 清冷仙子，月白流仙裙。身后伴有通体由白光凝聚、散发柔光的玉兔虚像，氛围空灵。
5. 辰龙（金）： 位居高位，玄色龙鳞袍，尊贵非凡。背后盘绕着延绵百丈、威严神圣的巨龙灵光虚像。
6. 巳蛇（火）： 魅惑秘术师，紫色蛇纹缎面袍。身后游走着细长深邃、由紫色流光构成的灵蛇虚像。
7. 午马（火）： 飒爽剑修，朱红劲装。身后是四蹄踏火、正欲奔腾的烈马光影虚像。
8. 未羊（土）： 温婉医修，米白棉麻仙裙。身后显现着神态祥和、如瑞云般朦胧的白羊光态虚像。
9. 申猴（金）： 桀骜斗战真人，战损金甲。身后是手持神兵、傲视天地的灵猴光影虚像。
10. 酉鸡（金）： 晨曦守望者，羽状剪裁战袍。身后双翼展开，现出流金溢彩、宛如虚像的锦凰光影。
11. 戌狗（土）： 忠诚将领，皮革金属轻铠。背后是昂首挺立、充满守护感的灵犬光影虚像。
12. 亥猪（水）： 极左侧灵泉旁。悠闲散仙，青色宽大袍服。身后萦绕着福泽深厚、由浑厚气韵构成的灵猪虚像。

最终愿景
这不再是孤立的个体，而是十二位生肖神祇在统一仙境中的史诗集结。通过“真人本体+背后灵光虚像”的视觉结构，完美平衡人的情感美感与生肖的神话底蕴，构建出极致的东方玄幻宇宙。
```

### 71. 超现实概念产品广告：助眠药“PILLow”

**Author**: [Nano banana pro🍌](https://x.com/Vishnudxe)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: en

> 一个用于为虚构安眠药“PILLow”生成极简主义概念广告静物画的提示。画面中，一个超大的琥珀色玻璃瓶将微型、毛绒、绗缝枕头倾泻到哑光蓝色表面上，强调超现实主义、干净的商业照明以及用于品牌宣传的清晰留白。

![超现实概念产品广告：助眠药“PILLow”](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977257576_7k95ul_G_HesMUXEAEKZ-L.jpg)

```
Minimalist advertising still life featuring an oversized amber glass supplement bottle tipped on its side, open black cap placed nearby. The bottle label reads “Use for Charging” in clean modern typography. From the bottle opening, several small white pillows spill out onto a smooth matte blue surface, arranged organically as if poured.

The pillows are soft, rectangular, quilted, and plush, resembling miniature ergonomic bed pillows. Strong visual contrast between the dark amber glass, crisp white pillows, and muted blue background.

Composition: top-down / three-quarter angle product shot, bottle positioned in the upper left, pillows scattered diagonally across the frame toward the lower right. Clear negative space at the bottom for branding text "PILLow".

Lighting: studio lighting with soft directional shadows, high clarity, subtle reflections on glass, controlled highlights.
Style: modern commercial product photography, surreal conceptual advertising aesthetic.
Color palette: deep blue background, warm amber glass, white textiles, black accents.
Mood: calm, clever, restful, contemporary.
Quality cues: ultra-sharp focus, high resolution, professional advertising campaign look.

Optional Negative Prompt

cluttered scene, harsh lighting, plastic texture, low contrast, messy shadows, distorted text, unrealistic materials
```

**Author**: [MAX](https://x.com/maxxmalist)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: en

asked claude for a hyperdetailed prompt 
- added 'vitiligo skin' to it
- generated first frame images in nano banana pro
- animated it in VEO

for character consistency across multiple generations, extract the face and use it as a reference image in Nano Banana Pro
```

### 79. 草图转 CAD 风格线条艺术转换提示

**Author**: [シャポコ🌵](https://x.com/shapoco)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: ja

> 一个用于 Nano Banana Pro（使用其“思考模式”）的两部分提示序列，可将粗略草图转换为精确的、类似 CAD 的线条艺术。第一个提示指示模型根据蓝色文本注释完成粗略草图，消除歧义，并应用线条粗细变化。第二个提示是后续指令，将相同的样式应用于后续的粗略草图。

![草图转 CAD 风格线条艺术转换提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977349240_zl2up0_G_G7Mn_WkAERemX.jpg)
![草图转 CAD 风格线条艺术转换提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977349222_i4r1qx_G_G7Nf4WsAE3C7S.jpg)
![草图转 CAD 风格线条艺术转换提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977349306_jgm0on_G_G7KWkWYAAWR54.jpg)
![草图转 CAD 风格线条艺术转换提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977350687_xdga71_G_G7OG2XAAE2qqL.jpg)

```
このラフ画を清書して線画を作って下さい。青い文字を読んで参考にし、手書きに伴う曖昧さや雑さは排除し、CADツールから出力したような精緻な線画にしてください。稜線は太くするなど、線の太さに強弱をつけてください。青い文字と線は削除し、出力画像には含めないでください

同じ調子でこのラフも清書してください
```

[[Technical Illustration]]

### 83. 超逼真巴西热带阳台肖像提示词

**Author**: [Nano banana pro🍌](https://x.com/Vishnudxe)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超逼真的年轻女性全身肖像，背景是阳光普照的阳台和郁郁葱葱的热带风光。该提示详细说明了身体特征、服装（热带比基尼上衣和超短迷你裙）、自信的姿势以及技术相机设置，以实现高对比度、逆光、8K 分辨率并充满热带度假氛围的图像。

![超逼真巴西热带阳台肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977285165_kvm7br_G_Gszi_WMAANhWO.jpg)

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "description": "An ultra-photorealistic, full-body portrait of young woman standing on a sunlit balcony with a lush tropical background.",
    "subject": {
      "demographics": "Young female adult, appearing in her early 20s.",
      "hair": "Long, voluminous, dark brown straight hair, parted to the side and cascading heavily over the right shoulder, backlit by the sun.",
      "skin": " deeply faired, sun-kissed complexion with visible tan lines around the bikini area, highlighting a summer glow.",
      "physique": "Fit, hourglass figure with a toned midriff.",
      "face": "Soft facial features with defined eyebrows, plump lips, and a sultry, neutral expression maintaining direct eye contact.",
      "clothing": {
        "top": "{argument name="bikini top color" default="Green and white"} botanical/tropical print string bikini top.",
        "bottom": "Low-rise, micro-mini wrap skirt in a textured, light beige/grey woven fabric.",
        "accessories": "Layered delicate necklaces including one with turquoise beads, silver bracelets on both wrists, and minimal rings."
      },
      "pose": "Leaning back casually against a waist-high white concrete balcony wall. Both arms are extended to the sides resting on the ledge, creating an open, confident posture. Hips are slightly swayed."
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "An outdoor hotel or resort balcony overlooking a tropical landscape.",
      "background": "Lush green trees and foliage filling the mid-ground. In the distance, a white resort building with a dark tiled roof is visible. The sky is bright blue with scattered white clouds.",
      "foreground": "Clean, white stucco balcony wall.",
      "framing": "Shot from slightly below eye level, capturing the subject from mid-thigh up to the top of the head, framed by the balcony overhang at the top."
    },
    "lighting": {
      "source": "Strong natural sunlight coming from behind and slightly to the left (backlighting).",
      "effect": "Creates a glowing rim light effect on her hair and shoulders (halo effect). The subject's face and front are in soft, open shade but illuminated by ambient bounce light. High contrast between the bright sky and the shadowed foreground.",
      "shadows": "Natural shadows cast on the midriff and under the neck."
    },
    "mood": {
      "vibe": "Tropical vacation, relaxed, confident, sultry, summery, luxurious.",
      "atmosphere": "Warm and breezy."

### 87. 使用 Nano Banana Pro 制作 Dan Koe 风格演示文稿（PPT）的终极提示

**Author**: [ナマケモノai](https://x.com/akaoji39)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: ja

> 一个高度详细、多步骤的系统提示，旨在将文章或文本（如 Dan Koe 的作品）转化为 10-15 页的演示文稿脚本，并为 Nano Banana Pro 生成相应的图像提示。风格指南要求采用高对比度、单色、蚀刻/雕刻美学，重点关注存在主义、未知以及渺小人类与巨大元素之间对比的主题。

![使用 Nano Banana Pro 制作 Dan Koe 风格演示文稿（PPT）的终极提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977364402_jouxh7_G_GfoTWWMAA8del.jpg)
![使用 Nano Banana Pro 制作 Dan Koe 风格演示文稿（PPT）的终极提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977364096_xwqm3j_G_GfoT2WUAAiI4g.jpg)
![使用 Nano Banana Pro 制作 Dan Koe 风格演示文稿（PPT）的终极提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977364269_mwhkkl_G_GfoTgXMAAklLK.jpg)
![使用 Nano Banana Pro 制作 Dan Koe 风格演示文稿（PPT）的终极提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977366015_omcqu6_G_GfoTeW8AAxo3w.jpg)

```
あなたは「Dan Koeスタイルの記事用画像 + 極限まで削ぎ落とした認知系PPT」制作者です。
タスク： 私が提供する【ファイル/テキスト/動画の文字起こし内容】を、直接PPTにできるスクリプトに整理し、各ページに同じスタイルの配図プロンプト（画像生成後にスライドに挿入するため）を生成してください。
目標とする気質： 孤独、探求、実存主義、未知の深淵、極限まで削ぎ落としているが力強い；白黒の高コントラスト、版画的線画、密集したハッチング陰影、巨大な未知 + 小さな人間。
【出力言語】日本語を主体とし、必要に応じて少量の英語キーワードを追加可（配図プロンプト用）。
【ページ数】{argument name="page count" default="10–15"}ページ（内容に応じて調整）。
【画面規格】16:9；各ページは**上部に横長バナー画像（画像内に要約テキストを含む）**を配置。
【スライドの原則】

そのスライドを見るだけで、何について話しているか8割理解できること
タイトルは具体的な主張・結論・問いかけであること（抽象的な単語のみは禁止）
3-5つのbulletで文脈が完結すること

【レイアウトルール】

各ページで1つの見解のみを語る
タイトル≤15文字：具体的な主張や問いの形式（例：「専門性の罠」「なぜ今、複数のスキルか」）
画像内に3–5つのbullet、各bullet≤18文字
画像外（スライド下部）に：60-120字程度の「補足説明」
全体で統一：白黒、余白、抑制、鋭利

【配図スタイルの固定（各ページで使用）】

pen-and-ink illustration / ink engraving / vintage etching
monochrome black & white, high contrast
extreme micro-detail linework
layered cross-hatching (3–5 layers) + stippling
scratchboard texture, paper grain
dramatic chiaroscuro lighting, deep shadows, rich midtones, crisp highlights
perfect pure black negative-space void（穴/ブラックホール/扉/深淵）を視覚的なアンカーポイントとして
tiny human/astronaut silhouette vs gigantic unknown

【統一ネガティブワード（各ページの配図プロンプト末尾に追加）】 NEGATIVE: color, grayscale photo, realistic photography, soft airbrush, smooth shading, blur, low detail, flat lighting, cartoon, anime, cel shading, watermark, logo, credit, UI, frame
【コンテンツ生成フロー】
まず7–9つの要点で原内容の「核心論点チェーン」を要約（論理順序に従って）

それを10–15ページのPPT構造にマッピング：表紙（1ページ）
現状/問題提起（1ページ）
鍵となる洞察（1ページ）
コアフレームワーク（2ページ）
方法とステップ（2–3ページ）
ケース/対比（1–2ページ）
よくある誤解（1ページ）
アクションチェックリスト（1ページ）
締めの金言（1ページ）

各ページの出力は必ず以下の形式に厳密に従って提供：

【Slide X：タイトル（具体的な主張・問い）】
画像内に表示するテキスト：
[具体的で分かりやすいタイトル：15文字以内]

- [要点1：何について話しているか分かる具体的な内容：18文字以内]
- [要点2：18文字以内]
- [要点3：18文字以内]
- [要点4：18文字以内]（オプション）
補足説明（スライド下部、60-120字）：[このスライドの背景や具体例を簡潔に説明。一人称で語りかけるように。]
配図Prompt（以下の形式を厳守）：
A 16:9 horizontal pen-and-ink illustration. [シーンの詳細を80-120字で描写：場所、人物の状態、巨大な要素、光と影]. 

THE BOTTOM 15-20% OF THE IMAGE MUST BE A SOLID BLACK HORIZONTAL BAR.
This black bar contains white Japanese text:
- Title (centered): "[上記のタイトルをそのまま記載]"
- Bullets (left-aligned):
  • "[bullet 1をそのまま記載]"
  • "[bullet 2をそのまま記載]"
  • "[bullet 3をそのまま記載]"
  [• "[bullet 4をそのまま記載]" (if applicable)]

Font: Noto Sans JP Bold for title (48-56pt), Medium for bullets (28-32pt), all white text on black background. No logo, no credit, no watermark.

Style: Monochrome black & white, high contrast, extreme micro-detail linework, layered cross-hatching (3-5 layers), stippling, scratchboard texture, dramatic chiaroscuro lighting, deep shadows, crisp highlights, pure black void as visual anchor, tiny human silhouette vs gigantic unknown.

NEGATIVE: color, grayscale photo, realistic photography, soft airbrush, smooth shading, blur, low detail, flat lighting, cartoon, anime, cel shading, watermark, logo, credit, UI, frame
配図構図提案：
主体：[位置と状態]
未知の要素：[配置]

光源：[方向]

必須：下部15-20%に黒バー＋白文字テキスト
【表紙の特別ルール】 タイトルはメインテーマを具体的に示す（例：「多重興味が新時代の超能力である理由」） サブタイトルまたは3-4つの
```

[[AI Workflow]] [[Presentation Design]]

- illustrated with fine graphite and ink cross-hatching
- layered with transparent tissue overlays showing bone and muscle
- on yellowing/ greying parchment paper

- Do not draw the subject twice - *only once*
- Do not skip some body parts - be complete
- No text at all

### 107. 超精细立体纸艺城市

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-19  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多层系统指令提示，旨在生成一张超详细、逼真的弹出式纸质城市图像，该城市从一张折叠地图中浮现，并指定了纸张纹理、有限的调色板以及倾斜移位微缩效果等相机效果。

```

1) Semantic Profiling (4 layers): Skyline / Transit / Nature / Population

2) Container:
- A large folded map opened into a cross shape.
- The city pops up via paper hinges, tabs, and accordion folds.

3) Palette:
- Everything is paper: textured cardstock, newsprint, vellum overlays
- Limited inks: 2–3 spot colors max + black linework
- Optional: gold foil accents ONLY for the title and key routes

4) Density:
- “Maximum papercraft density”: tiny cutout balconies, signage tabs, window punch-outs
- Transit represented as paper strips and dotted lines, with tiny vehicles as folded micro-forms
- Nature becomes layered contour lines and stacked paper topography

5) Typography:
- Title printed as a bold cartographic label integrated into the map legend
- Landmark names as tiny map callouts with leader lines

6) Camera/Light:
- Soft daylight, slight paper shadows, crisp edges, tilt-shift miniature vibe
Output: 1 image, 1:1, ultra-detailed papercraft realism.
```

[[Tilt-Shift Photography]] [[Miniature City]]

---

### 109. 诗歌推荐系统提示（雕刻书雕塑美学）

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-19  **Language**: en

> 一个多阶段提示，旨在充当文学策展人，分析一位诗人（例如 T.S. 艾略特），以寻找相似的国际诗人，然后根据他们的作品生成一个 2x2 的风景网格。视觉风格非常独特：一种雕刻书纸雕塑美学，风景从书页中浮现，诗歌的关键诗句被雕刻到地形中，并包含诗人的微型雕像。

![诗歌推荐系统提示（雕刻书雕塑美学）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890693989_xmf1d4_G-6ry6UWwAAsSTN.jpg)

```
TS Eliot -> Prompt: Role: Literary Curator & Typewriter Sculptor
Input: [Poet or Poem, e.g., {argument name="poet name" default="T.S. Eliot"}, Pablo Neruda]
Phase 1: Poetic Voice Analysis
Identify the poet's signature rhythm, recurring imagery, and emotional core.
Find 4 much less known international poets with similar styles and imagery and their best work
Extract 5-8 physical objects mentioned repeatedly in their work
Phase 2: Visual Execution
Goal: a 2x2 grid of 4 landscapes with this prompt. Carved book paper sculpture aesthetic, a repurposed hardcover book, [scene for each work emerging from the pages], [with words as part of the texture], intricate layered paper cuts, a monochromatic palette of aged paper, soft, raking light creating deep shadows, sculptural book as art object.

Rules per Panel:

The Transformation: The typed text physically rises from the page, forming a 3D topographical landscape
The Words: Key lines from the poem carved into the terrain like engraved stone
The Symbols: Miniature objects from the poem placed in the landscape (tiny boat, rose, clock, door)
The Poet: Microscopic figurine of the poet wandering through their own words
The Mood: Lighting matches emotional tone (fog for melancholy, harsh light for anger, soft gold for longing)
The Metadata: Name "Poet | Collection | Year"   poet and poet era relevant items in the background.
Output: 2x2 Grid, Macro Photography, shallow depth of field
```

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成名为“结晶的忧郁”的超现实电影叙事肖像。它描绘了一个主体置身于前卫冰雕师的工作室中，强调高负空间、穿透冰块的体积青色光线、实用的霜冻妆效，以及特定的中画幅相机设置（哈苏 H6D-100c），以呈现触觉、真实的纹理。

![结晶的忧郁：冰雕师工作室](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890663530_f5fv8x_G_Ag2U3WsAAcRqH.jpg)

```
{
  "vibe_title_en": "Crystallized Melancholy",
  "master_prompt": "A hyper-realistic, cinematic portrait of The Protagonist captured in a high-concept 'Ice Sculptor's Atelier.' The composition strictly follows the rule of thirds, placing the subject on the far right, leaving vast negative space filled with translucent, suspended blocks of raw ice and freezing mist. The subject is looking down and away with a soft, vulnerable expression, captured in the fragile moment of exhaling, with a visible plume of breath vapor hanging in the air. Practical effect makeup creates the illusion of frost crystallizing on the cheekbones and collarbone; hair is styled with a 'wet-frozen' stiff texture. Lighting involves cool cyan ambient light passing through the ice blocks to create volumetric rays, contrasted with a soft, focused white beam on the face. Shot on a Hasselblad H6D-100c with an 80mm f/1.9 lens for extremely shallow depth of field, focusing sharply on the skin texture while blurring the icy background. The image has the color grading of Fujifilm Pro 400H, emphasizing cool teals and silvers with organic film grain. No CGI fantasy; aesthetic is 'High-End Editorial Surrealism' with tangible, physical textures.",
  "meta": {
    "intent": "Editorial Fashion / Narrative Portraiture",

    "device_profile": "Medium Format Digital (Hasselblad)"
  },

    "aspect": "16:9",
    "composition": "Rule of Thirds, High Negative Space",

  },
  "subject": {

    "identity": "The Protagonist (Universal Template)",
    "demographics": "Adult, ethereal presence",

    "hair": "Wet-look styling, stiffened tips to mimic freezing",
    "body": "Shoulders visible, slight shiver posture",

  },

        "item": "Couture Gown",

### 157. Frank Miller《罪恶之城》图像小说风格迁移

**Author**: [Dominus the Prompter](https://x.com/iamdomprompt)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: en

> 一个旨在将上传图片中的主体转化为弗兰克·米勒 (Frank Miller) 的《罪恶之城》(Sin City) 系列漫画中那种鲜明、高对比度美学风格的提示词。它要求深邃的阴影、密集的交叉影线、粗重的墨线轮廓，以及在虚空背景下戏剧性的明暗对比光效。

![Frank Miller《罪恶之城》图像小说风格迁移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890739480_1d3phh_G-9u8TdXkAENVpG.jpg)

```
The subjects from the uploaded image rendered in a stark, high-contrast graphic novel style, heavily inspired by Frank Miller's Sin City aesthetic. Deep, unforgiving shadows define the muscular structure and harsh expressions, utilizing heavy cross-hatching and thick ink outlines instead of traditional shading. Dramatic chiaroscuro lighting emphasizes the tension between the two figures, with only stark white highlights cutting through the predominantly black composition, against a pure void background, appearing like a single, powerful comic book panel.
```

> 一个高度具体的提示，用于生成一张以随机选定的官方三丽鸥 (Sanrio) 角色为主题的单张大阿卡那塔罗牌。该提示要求将角色与一个随机的十二星座主题相结合，并将最终图像渲染为超详细的孔版印刷 (risograph) 模拟效果，重点突出真实的纹理、随机点状网点 (stochastic dot stippling) 和大胆、平坦的专色。

![Sanrio 塔罗牌孔版印刷模拟](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804325037_1z9f6f_G-9V68nX0AAHE3P.jpg)
![Sanrio 塔罗牌孔版印刷模拟](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804325245_mf7i75_G-uNF-ZXQAAKbIH.jpg)

The character must be depicted with 100% canonical accuracy maintaining exact official Sanrio proportions and features, positioned centrally as the card's main subject in a pose that embodies the tarot card's archetypal meaning. The entire composition must be a high-quality risograph print simulation featuring authentic soy-based ink grain texture that mimics absorption on uncoated 80-120gsm paper stock, stochastic dot stippling using randomized diffusion dither patterns (not regular halftone grids), fine sand-like noise within all color fills simulating Grain Touch screening mode, organic ink density variations creating tonal shifts without smooth gradients, slight dot gain effect at color boundaries, and spot color separation logic with translucent ink layering behavior rather than CMYK process colors. The border design should use a maximum of 3-4 spot colors plus black, with the character surrounded by a thick uniform black outline (3-4pt stroke weight). Background within the border should be cream/off-white (#FFF8E7) to simulate aged tarot card stock. The output must be 3000×5200px resolution in sRGB, containing absolutely no text labels, character names, tarot card titles, zodiac symbols (♈♉♊♋♌♍♎♏♐♑♒♓), Roman numerals, descriptive typography, or dimensional effects like drop shadows.

### 176. 烹饪科学立体模型：巧克力的化学

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂、结构化的提示，用于生成一张“烹饪科学”立体模型照片，特别展示巧克力或焦糖等食物的化学原理。场景中有一个 L 形展示盒、一个带有培养皿中样本的元素周期表背景、一个 1:12 比例的科学家模型，以及由食物本身制成的巨大 3D 挤压字母，以“韦斯·安德森”式的对称风格呈现。

![烹饪科学立体模型：巧克力的化学](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804323526_yo8sqc_G-1VmdxWgAAhdsk.jpg)
![烹饪科学立体模型：巧克力的化学](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804323346_v3d1rj_G-1VmdqW0AA6LfW.jpg)

```
do this for {argument name="Food Item" default="caramel"} <instruction>
 
Input A is a Complex Food Item or Dish (e.g., Chocolate, Bread, Cheese, Coffee).
Deconstruct the subject into   3 Scientific Layers  :
     The States of Matter:  Identify 4–5 stages of processing.
         (e.g., Cocoa Bean -> Nibs -> Liquor -> Powder. Wheat -> Flour -> Dough -> Crumb). 
     The Texture Samples:  Identify the physical properties to display as swatches.
         (e.g., Snap/Gloss for Chocolate. Porosity/Crust for Bread. Rind/Creaminess for Cheese). 
     The Material: Identify the substance for the 3D text.
         (e.g., Molded Dark Chocolate, Baked Bread Crust, Hard Wax/Cheese). 

  2. Container: 
Goal: "Culinary Science" Diorama Photography.
     The Stage:  An   L-Shaped Display Box   (Vertical Backboard + Horizontal Floor).
     The Finish:  Clean, matte Cream or White plastic, resembling a high-end educational kit or museum exhibit.
     The Frame:  A simple wooden or plastic border framing the scene.

  3. Periodic Table background: 
     The Grid:  The vertical wall features a neat, symmetrical grid of circular   Petri Dishes or Ceramic Bowls  .
     The Contents:  Each dish contains a sample of the "States of Matter" (Step 1).
     The Swatches:  Below the dishes are square tiles displaying the "Texture Samples" (e.g., a square of perfectly tempered chocolate next to a bloomed one).
     The Labels:  Tiny, legible scientific text (Serif font) printed directly on the wall under each sample.

  4. The Floor (The Laboratory):  
     The Narrative:  A 1:12 scale   Scientist or Chef   figure (wearing a lab coat) stands at a central wooden workbench.
    Equipment:  The desk is cluttered with a mix of   Chemistry Glassware   (Beakers, Flasks) and   Culinary Tools   (Whisks, Scales).
     The Experiment:  The figure is actively testing or measuring the food product.

  5. Typography : 
     Placement:  Massive, thick   3D Extruded Letters   stand on the very front edge of the floor, acting as a barrier.
     Construction:  The letters are made  of  the food itself (e.g., "THE CHEMISTRY OF CHOCOLATE" molded in dark chocolate).
     Text:  "THE CHEMISTRY OF {argument name="Input A" default="CHOCOLATE"}".

  Output:   ONE image, 1:1 Aspect Ratio, Studio Product Lighting, "Wes Anderson" Symmetry, Educational Aesthetic.
</instruction>
```

### 181. 北极探险家特写肖像

### 200. 详细写实角色扮演肖像提示：凤凰主题

**Author**: [行者AI视频](https://x.com/joshesye)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: zh

> 一个高度详细、照片级的图像生成提示，用于创建基于游戏《王者荣耀》中“凤凰”主题的女性角色 Cosplay 肖像。该提示详细说明了构图、灯光设计（专业影棚设置，带彩色 LED 舞台灯）、艺术风格（高清晰度的现代写实主义）、配色方案（红色、金色、白色，具有冷暖对比）以及服装和场景的复杂视觉细节。

![详细写实角色扮演肖像提示：凤凰主题](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804326821_r6ye12_G-7ReqTXQAAyLxF.jpg)

```
这张极其细腻的高清摄影人像捕捉了一位身着华丽《王者荣耀》凤凰主题服饰的女性角色扮演者。

**构图与姿势：** 采用垂直的中景全身构图，主角居中，身体微侧。她右手轻捏一把橘红色的羽毛扇，左手斜持一柄精致的金色凤凰权杖，权杖顶端镶嵌着发光的球体。动态的站姿结合略微俯拍的视角，增强了角色的优雅感与气场。

**光影设计：** 画面呈现出专业的摄影棚级光效。上方的大型柔光箱提供了均匀、细腻的前向照明，完美勾勒出人物的面部轮廓与皮肤质感。地面上排列着数个彩色LED舞台射灯，散发出蓝、紫、红的多色光芒，为背景和地面投射出动感且富有层次的色彩。

**艺术风格：** 现代写实摄影风格，具有极高的清晰度和色彩饱和度。画面融合了游戏艺术的幻想感与商业人像摄影的精致感，细节锐利，呈现出电影质感的角色写照。

**配色方案：** 核心配色由华丽的朱红、亮金和纯白组成。服饰裙摆呈现出从金黄到橘红再到深紫的渐变羽毛纹理。背景以深紫色和靛蓝色的展会海报为基调，与角色温暖的红金主色调形成鲜明的冷暖对比，使主体脱颖而出。

**视觉细节：** 主角拥有如瀑般的银白色长卷发，头戴镶嵌红宝石的金色镂空冠冕。服装细节极其考究，包括白色的羽毛胸饰、红色的天鹅绒质感面料，以及层叠的金色金属护甲。背景中若隐若现的展会人群和游戏标识增加了环境的真实感和叙事深度。
```
